# 🔢 800 Solved Aptitude Questions

This file contains exactly 800 solved quantitative, logical, and verbal aptitude questions mirroring the TCS NQT distribution.

### Q1. If the price of an item is Rs. 60 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 60
  - B) Rs. 72.0
  - C) Rs. 65
  - D) Rs. 120
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 72.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 60 * (1 + 20/100) = 60 * 1.2 = 72.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q2. A can complete a task in 9 days and B can do it in 10 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 4.74 days
  - B) 19 days
  - C) 9 days
  - D) 10 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 4.74 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (9 * 10) / (9 + 10) = 90 / 19 = 4.74 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q3. Convert a speed of 144 km/h into m/s.
* **Options**:
  - A) 40 m/s
  - B) 144 m/s
  - C) 288 m/s
  - D) 0 m/s
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 40 m/s  
  **Explanation**: Convert km/h to m/s by multiplying by 5/18: 144 * 5/18 = 40 m/s.  
  **Trick**: Multiply directly by 5/18.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q4. Find the Simple Interest on Rs. 900 at 10% p.a. for 2 years.
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 180
  - B) Rs. 190
  - C) Rs. 360
  - D) Rs. 900
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) Rs. 180  
  **Explanation**: SI = (P * R * T) / 100 = (900 * 10 * 2) / 100 = 180.  
  **Trick**: Calculate 10% of principal and multiply by years.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q5. What is the remainder when 103 is divided by 9?
* **Options**:
  - A) 4
  - B) 5
  - C) 6
  - D) 0
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 4  
  **Explanation**: Divide 103 by 9: 103 = 9 * 11 + 4. The remainder is 4.  
  **Trick**: Sum the digits to find the remainder of 9 divisibility.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q7. A can complete a task in 14 days and B can do it in 15 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 7.24 days
  - B) 29 days
  - C) 14 days
  - D) 15 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 7.24 days

  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q51. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q96. If the price of an item is Rs. 210 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 210
  - B) Rs. 252.0
  - C) Rs. 215
  - D) Rs. 420
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 252.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 210 * (1 + 20/100) = 210 * 1.2 = 252.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q97. A can complete a task in 24 days and B can do it in 15 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?

  - C) 24 days
  - D) 15 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 9.23 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (24 * 15) / (24 + 15) = 360 / 39 = 9.23 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

  - B) Rs. 72.0
  - C) Rs. 65
  - D) Rs. 120
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 72.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 60 * (1 + 20/100) = 60 * 1.2 = 72.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q191. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q236. If the price of an item is Rs. 210 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 210
  - B) Rs. 252.0
  - C) Rs. 215
  - D) Rs. 420
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 252.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 210 * (1 + 20/100) = 210 * 1.2 = 252.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q237. A can complete a task in 24 days and B can do it in 20 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?

  - C) 24 days
  - D) 20 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 10.91 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (24 * 20) / (24 + 20) = 480 / 44 = 10.91 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q331. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q471. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q472. A can complete a task in 19 days and B can do it in 15 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?

  - C) 19 days
  - D) 15 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 8.38 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (19 * 15) / (19 + 15) = 285 / 34 = 8.38 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

  - A) 5
  - B) 6
  - C) 7
  - D) 0
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 5  
  **Explanation**: Divide 203 by 9: 203 = 9 * 22 + 5. The remainder is 5.  
  **Trick**: Sum the digits to find the remainder of 9 divisibility.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q516. If the price of an item is Rs. 210 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 210
  - B) Rs. 252.0
  - C) Rs. 215
  - D) Rs. 420
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 252.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 210 * (1 + 20/100) = 210 * 1.2 = 252.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q517. A can complete a task in 24 days and B can do it in 15 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 9.23 days
  - B) 39 days
  - C) 24 days
  - D) 15 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 9.23 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (24 * 15) / (24 + 15) = 360 / 39 = 9.23 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q518. Convert a speed of 414 km/h into m/s.
* **Options**:
  - A) 115 m/s
  - B) 414 m/s
  - C) 828 m/s
  - D) 0 m/s
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 115 m/s  
  **Explanation**: Convert km/h to m/s by multiplying by 5/18: 414 * 5/18 = 115 m/s.  
  **Trick**: Multiply directly by 5/18.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q519. Find the Simple Interest on Rs. 2400 at 10% p.a. for 2 years.
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 480
  - B) Rs. 490
  - C) Rs. 960
  - D) Rs. 2400
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) Rs. 480  
  **Explanation**: SI = (P * R * T) / 100 = (2400 * 10 * 2) / 100 = 480.  
  **Trick**: Calculate 10% of principal and multiply by years.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q611. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q612. A can complete a task in 19 days and B can do it in 20 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 9.74 days
  - B) 39 days
  - C) 19 days
  - D) 20 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 9.74 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (19 * 20) / (19 + 20) = 380 / 39 = 9.74 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q656. If the price of an item is Rs. 210 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 210
  - B) Rs. 252.0
  - C) Rs. 215
  - D) Rs. 420
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 252.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 210 * (1 + 20/100) = 210 * 1.2 = 252.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q657. A can complete a task in 24 days and B can do it in 20 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 10.91 days
  - B) 44 days
  - C) 24 days
  - D) 20 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 10.91 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (24 * 20) / (24 + 20) = 480 / 44 = 10.91 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q706. If the price of an item is Rs. 110 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 110
  - B) Rs. 132.0
  - C) Rs. 115
  - D) Rs. 220
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 132.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 110 * (1 + 20/100) = 110 * 1.2 = 132.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

### Q751. If the price of an item is Rs. 160 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 160
  - B) Rs. 192.0
  - C) Rs. 165
  - D) Rs. 320
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 192.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 160 * (1 + 20/100) = 160 * 1.2 = 192.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q752. A can complete a task in 19 days and B can do it in 10 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:

  - B) 29 days
  - C) 19 days
  - D) 10 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 6.55 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (19 * 10) / (19 + 10) = 190 / 29 = 6.55 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 5  
  **Explanation**: Divide 203 by 9: 203 = 9 * 22 + 5. The remainder is 5.  
  **Trick**: Sum the digits to find the remainder of 9 divisibility.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q796. If the price of an item is Rs. 210 and it is increased by 20%, what is the new price?
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 210
  - B) Rs. 252.0
  - C) Rs. 215
  - D) Rs. 420
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: B) Rs. 252.0  
  **Explanation**: New price = 210 * (1 + 20/100) = 210 * 1.2 = 252.0.  
  **Trick**: Add 10% of value (which is divide by 10) twice: 10% is {val/10}, twice is {val/5}. Add to base.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q797. A can complete a task in 24 days and B can do it in 10 days. Working together, in how many days can they complete it?
* **Options**:
  - A) 7.06 days
  - B) 34 days
  - C) 24 days
  - D) 10 days
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 7.06 days  
  **Explanation**: Together time = (A * B) / (A + B) = (24 * 10) / (24 + 10) = 240 / 34 = 7.06 days.  
  **Trick**: Use combined efficiency formula directly.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q798. Convert a speed of 414 km/h into m/s.
* **Options**:
  - A) 115 m/s
  - B) 414 m/s
  - C) 828 m/s
  - D) 0 m/s
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 115 m/s  
  **Explanation**: Convert km/h to m/s by multiplying by 5/18: 414 * 5/18 = 115 m/s.  
  **Trick**: Multiply directly by 5/18.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q799. Find the Simple Interest on Rs. 2400 at 10% p.a. for 2 years.
* **Options**:
  - A) Rs. 480
  - B) Rs. 490
  - C) Rs. 960
  - D) Rs. 2400
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) Rs. 480  
  **Explanation**: SI = (P * R * T) / 100 = (2400 * 10 * 2) / 100 = 480.  
  **Trick**: Calculate 10% of principal and multiply by years.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>

---

### Q800. What is the remainder when 53 is divided by 9?
* **Options**:
  - A) 8
  - B) 0
  - C) 1
  - D) 0
* <details><summary>🔍 View Answer & Explanation</summary>

  **Correct Answer**: A) 8  
  **Explanation**: Divide 53 by 9: 53 = 9 * 5 + 8. The remainder is 8.  
  **Trick**: Sum the digits to find the remainder of 9 divisibility.  
  **Time to Solve**: 30 seconds.
  </details>
